draw_item_in_screenbuf:
T6C56h	3A40E7..  :@..	LD	A,(TE740H)		; A = item id
T6C59h	B7......  ....	OR	A			;
T6C5Ah	C8......  ....	RET	Z			; if(no item in room) return

T6C5Bh	FE07....  ....	CP	007h			; Compute A - 7 and set flags.
T6C5Dh	381D....  8...	JR	C,01Dh			; if(A<7) Jump to 06C7CH. i.e. jump if weapon, i.e. jump if half height
; Not a weapon/not half height
T6C5Fh	D62D....  .-..	SUB	02Dh			; A -= 0x2D
T6C61h	3013....  0...	JR	NC,013h			; if (A >= 0) Jump to 06C76H. I.e jump if arrow/coin/key.
; Just a normal item, full height (2x2 characters).
T6C63h	3E76....  >v..	LD	A,076h			; A = 0x76

; We can also come here from T6C7Ah, where A is set for arrow/key/coin.
T6C65h	2A44E7..  *D..	LD	HL,(TE744H)		; HL = top left position of screenbuffer of item.
T6C68h	77......  w...	LD	(HL),A			; Set top left to character 0x76
T6C69h	3C......  <...	INC	A			; ++A, A from 0x76 to 0x77
T6C6Ah	2C......  ,...	INC	L			; HL = top right position of screenbuffer of item.
T6C6Bh	77......  w...	LD	(HL),A			; Set top right to character 0x77
T6C6Ch	011F00..  ....	LD	BC,0001Fh		; BC = 0x1F (full line is 0x20)
T6C6Fh	09......  ....	ADD	HL,BC			; HL = bottom left position of screenbuffer of item.
T6C70h	3C......  <...	INC	A			; ++A, A from 0x77 to 0x78.
T6C71h	77......  w...	LD	(HL),A			; Set bottom left to character 0x78.
T6C72h	2C......  ,...	INC	L			; HL = bottom right position of screenbuffer of item.
T6C73h	3C......  <...	INC	A			; ++A, A from 0x78 to 0x79.
T6C74h	77......  w...	LD	(HL),A			; Set bottom right to character 0x79
T6C75h	C9......  ....	RET			

; Draw arrow/key/coin.
; A == 0: Arrow
; A == 1: Coin
; A == 2: Key

; Compute: A = 0x60 + 4 * A
; Results:
; Arrow: A == 0x60
; Coin:  A == 0x64
; Key:   A == 0x68
T6C76h	87......  ....	ADD	A,A			; A+=A
T6C77h	87......  ....	ADD	A,A			; A+=A
T6C78h	C660....  .`..	ADD	A,060h			; A+=0x60

T9FCFh	FE09....  ....	CP	009h		; VaseState==9 means vase must appear
T9FD1h	0E1B....  ....	LD	C,01Bh		; C = 0x1B Note: 0x1B is the item number of the vase.

T9FD6h	CA49A0..  .I..	JP	Z,TA049H	; if(VaseState==9) jump to 0xA049 (appear_item)
; 0 -> 1: player needs to face right and swing sword
; 1 -> 2: player needs to face right and swing sword again
; 2 -> 3: player needs to face right and swing sword again
; 3 -> 4: player needs to face left  and swing sword
; 4 -> 5: player needs to face left  and swing sword again
; 5 -> 6: player needs to face left  and swing sword again
; 6 -> 7: player needs to jump
; 7 -> 8: player needs to jump again
; 8 -> 8: player needs to jump again
T9FD9h	FE06....  ....	CP	006h		; Compute VaseState - 6 and set flags.
T9FDBh	3017....  0...	JR	NC,017h		; if(VaseState>=6) Jump to 0x9FF4
; We are in VaseState 0, 1, 2, 3, 4, 5: a sword fling is needed to advance.
T9FDDh	47......  G...	LD	B,A		; Save A in B.
T9FDEh	3A38E5..  :8..	LD	A,(TE538H)	; 0: Sword not flinging, 1: sword flings ?for 1 frame?
T9FE1h	A7......  ....	AND	A		;
T9FE2h	C8......  ....	RET	Z		; Sword not flinging: no reset

T9FE3h	78......  x...	LD	A,B		; A = VaseState
T9FE4h	FE03....  ....	CP	003h		; Compute A - 3 and set flags, C is set for A <= 2
T9FE6h	3F......  ?...	CCF			; Flip carry bit ("Complement Carry Flag"), NC for A <= 2, C is set for A >= 3.
T9FE7h	3A03E5..  :...	LD	A,(TE503H)	; 0: facing right, 1: facing left, 2: climbing
T9FEAh	3803....  8...	JR	C,003h		; if(VaseState > 3) jump to 0x9FEF.
T9FECh	A7......  ....	AND	A		; Set Z flag if facing right. (VaseState <= 2)
T9FEDh	1801....  ....	JR	001h		; Jump to 09FF0H unconditionally.

; We can only jump from T9FEAh to here, in which case the following hold: VaseState >= 3
T9FEFh	3D......  ....	DEC	A		; --A. New meaning: 0==facing left (Z), 1==climbing (NZ)

; We can also jump from T9FEDh to here.
; Jumped from T9FEDh:		Z flag is set if facing right, NZ if not facing right. VaseState: 0 or 1 or 2
; Fallthrough from T9FEFh:	Z flag is set if facing left,  NZ if not facing left.  VaseState: 3 or 4 or 5
T9FF0h	2052....  .R..	JR	NZ,052h		; if(not facing to correct side) Jump to 0A044H: reset_vase

T9FF7h	A7......  ....	AND	A			;
